City-API

City 요약 정보 조회

HTTP request

GET /api/v1/city/grid-infos HTTP/1.1
Accept: application/json
Host: api.liveamonth.com

HTTP response

HTTP/1.1 200 OK
Vary: Origin
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Method
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers
Content-Type: application/json
Content-Length: 1283

Response fields-data

Path Type Description

name.code

String

도시 코드

name.value

String

도시 이름

image

String

이미지 주소(uri)

averageDegree

Number

평균 기온

transportScore

Number

교통 점수

City 소개 정보 조회

HTTP request

GET /api/v1/city/BS HTTP/1.1
Accept: application/json
Host: api.liveamonth.com

Path parameter

Snippet path-parameter not found for operation::city-intro-get
